#新手教程
Use <u><b>WASD</b></u> to move.=使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 移動。
Use <u><b>WASD</b></u> on your keyboard until the progress bar is filled!=使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 按住鍵盤上的按鍵，直到進度條填滿！
Use <u><b>WASD</b></u> to move=使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 移動
Use <b><u>LEFT MOUSE + RIGHT MOUSE</b></u> to rotate an object you are holding=使用 <b><u>鼠標左鍵+鼠標右鍵</b></u> 旋轉你拿著的物品
<b>FOCUS > </b>Move to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>移動以填充進度條
<b>FOCUS > </b>Jump to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>跳躍以填充進度條
Press <u><b>SPACE</b></u> to jump.=按 <u><b>SPACE</b></u> 跳。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Sneak to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>蹲下填充進度條
Press <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> to sneak. Monsters are less likely to see you.=按 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 蹲下，怪物可能看不到你。
Hold <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> and use <u><b>WASD</b></u> until the progess is filled!=長按 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 和使用 <u><b>WASD</b></u> 直到進度完成！
Hold <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> and walk in under a prop, stay there until you fill the progress bar!=長按 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 然後走進物體下面，呆在那里，直到你填滿進度條！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Hide to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>躲藏以填充進度條
Use <u><b>CONTROL</b></u> to sneak under stuff and hide.=使用 <u><b>Ctrl</b></u> 偷偷溜到物體下面躲起來。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Sprint to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>沖刺以填充進度條
Hold down <u><b>LEFT SHIFT</b></u> to sprint. This drains your energy.=長按 <u><b>左 Shift</b></u> 沖刺，這會消耗你的耐力。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Run, jump and fall to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>奔跑、跳躍和翻滾以填充進度條
Run and press <u><b>Q</b></u> to fall with style. Jumping also helps!=奔跑並按下 <u><b>Q</b></u> 進行翻滾，也可以進行跳躍！
Run (<u><b>LEFT SHIFT</b></u>), jump (<u><b>SPACE</b></u>) and press <u><b>Q</b></u> to throw yourself. Do it until you fill the progress bar!=沖刺(<u><b>左 Shift</b></u>)，跳躍(<u><b>SPACE</b></u>)並按 <u><b>Q</b></u> 這樣做，直到你填滿進度條！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Carry that thing to fill the progress bar=<b>提示> </b>攜帶該物品以填充進度條
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) and hold it until you fill the progress bar!=抓取(<u><b>鼠標左鍵</b></u>)按住它，直到填滿進度條！
Grab objects using <u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>.=使用<u><b>鼠標左鍵</b></u>抓取物品.
<b>FOCUS > </b>Alter the distance of a grabbed item=<b>提示> </b>改變抓取物品的距離
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) an item and use <u><b>MOUSE SCROLL</b></u> to alter the distance of the item you grabbed!=抓住(<u><b>鼠標左鍵</b></u>)物品 <u><b>滾動鼠標</b></u> 改變你抓取的物品的距離！
Use <u><b>MOUSE SCROLL</b></u> to alter the distance of grabbed objects.=使用 <u><b>鼠標滾動</b></u> 以改變抓取物品的距離。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Rotate stuff to fill the progress bar.=<b>提示> </b>旋轉物品以填充進度條。
Rotate grabbed objects using <u><b>MOUSE RIGHT</b></u>.=使用以下按鍵旋轉抓取的物品 <u><b>鼠標右鍵</b></u>.
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) and hold it while you press <u><b>MOUSE RIGHT</b></u> and move your aim to rotate it. Rotate until you fill the progress bar!=抓住(<u><b>鼠標左鍵</b></u>)按住它，同時按下 <u><b>鼠標右鍵</b></u> 然後移動並旋轉它，旋轉直到填滿進度條！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Toggle that thing on and off.=<b>提示> </b>打開和關閉物品。
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) the ball and toggle it on and off using <u><b>E</b></u> until you fill the progress bar!=抓住(<u><b>鼠標左鍵</b></u>)然後使用以下按鍵打開和關閉球 <u><b>E</b></u> 直到你填滿進度條！
Grab and press <u><b>E</b></u> to toggle items.=抓取並按下 <u><b>E</b></u> 進行物品交互。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Fill your entire inventory.=<b>提示> </b>裝滿您的全部庫存。
Grab (<u><b>MOUSE LEFT</b></u>) an item, hold it and press <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u>. Fill all spots in your inventory to complete the progress bar!=抓住(<u><b>鼠標左鍵</b></u>)一個物品，按住它並按下 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u>鍵，裝滿庫存中的所有位置以完成進度條！
Grab an Item and use <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> to put it in your inventory.=抓取物品並按下 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> 鍵把它放在你的庫存中。
Use <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> and empty all spots to fill the progress bar!=使用 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> 並清空所有庫存以填充進度條！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Empty your entire inventory.=<b>提示> </b>清空您的全部庫存。
Use <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> to take items out of your inventory.=使用 <u><b>1</b></u>/<u><b>2</b></u>/<u><b>3</b></u> 從庫存中取出物品。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Check the map.=<b>提示> </b>查看地圖。
Use <u><b>TAB</b></u> to view the map. The map is <b><u>important</b></u> for navigation.=使用 <u><b>Tab</b></u> 查看地圖 <b><u>這很重要的</b></u>， 可用於導航。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Walk around with the C.A.R.T. a little.=<b>提示> </b>帶著推車四處走走。
This is a C.A.R.T. Grab it by the handle.=這是推車，抓住把手。
C.A.R.T.=推車
Mode: STRONG=模式：強
<b>FOCUS > </b>Fill the C.A.R.T. with valuables.=<b>提示> </b>把貴重物品裝滿推車。
Fill C.A.R.T.s with valuables. C.A.R.T.s are <b><u>important</b></u> for carrying more stuff.=把貴重物品裝滿推車，推車 <b><u>很重要</b></u> 能攜帶更多物品。
Mode: WEAK=模式：弱
Put three items into the C.A.R.T.=將三個物品放入推車。
<b>FOCUS > </b>Extract the valuables.=<b>提示> </b>取出貴重物品。
Activate and fill <b><u>Extraction Points</b></u> with valuables.=激活並裝滿<b><u>提取點</b></u> 貴重物品。
HELLO! FILL THE <b><u>EXTRACTION POINT</b></u> WITH VALUABLES!=你好！裝滿 <b><u>提取點</b></u> 貴重物品！
<b>FOCUS > </b>Fill the extraction point with valuables=<b>提示> </b>在提取點裝滿貴重物品

###############################3.15翻譯新增######################################################
REPO_HD=高清
Anti Aliasing=抗鋸齒
REPO Scanner=掃描儀
REPO Config=模組配置
Sturdier Valuables=更堅固的貴重物品
The number of times the upgrade item is applied at the start of the game.=升級物品在遊戲開始時應用的次數。
The maximum number of times the upgrade item can appear in the shop.=升級物品在商店中出現的最大次數。
The maximum number of times the upgrade item can be bought at once.=升級物品一次可購買的最大次數。
The initial delay (in seconds) before valuables begin scaling.=貴重物品開始縮放前的初始延遲（以秒為單位）。
The speed at which valuables scale down/up per update. Higher values make valuables shrink/expand faster.=貴重物品每次更新時縮放縮小/放大的速度。數值越高，貴重物品收縮/膨脹得越快。
Sets the time players have to kill a monster and get money when there aren’t enough items and the objectives are still pending.=當物品不足且目標仍未完成時，設置玩家擊殺怪物並獲得金錢的時間限制。
Ratio of Map Value to Extraction Goal. Ex: 20k map value to 10k goal is 2.0=地圖價值與提取目標的比例。例如：20k地圖價值對應10k目標為2.0。
The maximum number of health pacls the shop will spawn. Vanilla default: 3=商店生成的生命補給包的最大數量。原版默認值為3。
The maximum number of upgrades the shop will spawn. Vanilla default: 3=商店生成的升級物品的最大數量。原版默認值為3。
The maximum number of items the shop will spawn. Vanilla default: 8=商店生成的物品的最大數量。原版默認值為8。
How fast descriptions scroll. (Seconds per character)=描述滾動的速度。（每秒字符數）
Description Scroll Speed=描述滾動速度
The multiplier of how much value is deducted from a hit (lower is better)=擊中時價值扣除的倍數（越低越好）。
Damage Reduction Multiplier=傷害減免倍數。
Health amount deducted each time while crouching | 蹲下治療扣除自己的生命值=蹲下治療時每次扣除的生命值。
Health amount healed each time while crouching | 蹲下治療治療隊友的生命值=蹲下治療時每次治療隊友的生命值。
Interval for grab heal while crouching (in seconds) | 蹲下治療的間隔時間（秒）=蹲下治療的間隔時間（秒）。
You have more stamina, strength and can jump higher!\nPress R to continue=你擁有更多耐力、力量並能跳得更高！\n按R鍵繼續

Mage=法師
[H] Heal yourself for {{A}} health ({{B}} Mana)\n\n[N] Regenerate your stamina to full ({{C}} Mana)\n\n[J] Become faster for {{D}} seconds ({{E}} Mana)\n\n[O] Boost the effectivity of spells used in the next {{F}} seconds ({{G}} Mana)\n\n[K] Jump higher for {{H}} seconds ({{I}} Mana)=[H] 治療自己{{A}}點生命值（消耗{{B}}點法力）\n\n[N] 完全恢覆耐力（消耗{{C}}點法力）\n\n[J] 在{{D}}秒內提升速度（消耗{{E}}點法力）\n\n[O] 在接下來的{{F}}秒內提升法術效果（消耗{{G}}點法力）\n\n[K] 在{{H}}秒內跳得更高（消耗{{I}}點法力）

PowerMultiplier indicates how many times greater the current crystal energy is compared to the vanilla. eg) value set to 2 then the crystal energy that was originally sufficient for one device can now power two devices.=能量倍率表示當前晶體能量是原版能量的多少倍。例如，若值設置為2，則原本足夠供一台設備使用的晶體能量現在可供兩台設備使用。

[Host-only] Lower Value \= More Generous. A value of 0.5 will halve the impact when placing items into the cart, decreasing the likelihood of damaging an item. And a value of 1.0 will not reduce the impact at all, so be careful!=[僅限主機] 數值越低越寬松。值為0.5時，放入購物車時的影響減半，降低損壞物品的幾率。值為1.0時則完全不減少影響，請謹慎操作！

Sets healing value options to the same as in health packs, one of which will be applied randomly\rAttention! You must set the `PhaseMode` parameter to only one of `Level` or `Lobby`, not both. Otherwise, the healing will be done twice.\rIf the value is `None`, then it is disabled.\rIt has priority over the `Percent` and `ExactValue` parameters.\rFor example, if you set the value to `Medium, Large`, you will receive a random healing of 50HP or 100HP.\rSmall - heal 25 HP.\rMedium - heal 50 HP.\rLarge - heal 100 HP.=將治療值選項設為與醫療包相同，並隨機應用其中一種  \n注意！必須將 `PhaseMode` 參數僅設為 `Level` 或 `Lobby` 之一，不可同時設置，否則治療會生效兩次。  \n若值為 `None`，則禁用此功能。  \n該參數優先級高於 `Percent` 和 `ExactValue`。  \n例如：設為 `Medium, Large` 時，將隨機恢覆50HP或100HP。  \n- 小型：恢覆25HP  \n- 中型：恢覆50HP  \n- 大型：恢覆100HP

Sets the exact value to heal.\rAttention! You must set the `PhaseMode` parameter to only one of `Level` or `Lobby`, not both. Otherwise, the healing will be done twice.\rIf the value is `0`, then it is disabled.\rIt has priority over the `Percent` parameter.\rFor example, if you set the value to `15`, you will always receive 15 HP.=設置精確的治療數值。  \n注意！必須將 `PhaseMode` 參數僅設為 `Level` 或 `Lobby` 之一，不可同時設置，否則治療會生效兩次。  \n若值為 `0`，則禁用此功能。  \n該參數優先級高於 `Percent`。  \n例如：設為 `15` 時，將固定恢覆15HP。

Configures in which phases of the game health restoration will be triggered.\rLevel - when spawning in the level.\rShop - when spawning in the shop. Attention! Healing in the store does not affect the game.\rLobby - when spawning in the truck (not menu) before starting the next level.\rAll - in all phases.=配置遊戲在哪些階段觸發生命恢覆：  \n**關卡** - 進入關卡時；  \n**商店** - 進入商店時（注意：商店內恢覆不影響遊戲進程）；  \n**準備區** - 進入卡車（非菜單）準備下一關時；  \n**全部** - 所有階段均生效。

Configures the work mode.\rWarning: You are using `HostAndClient` value for this parameter at your own risk.\rIt may stop working after future game updates.\rIf another lobby players do not agree with this parameter, do not use it.\rAlso, the `Percent` parameter may not work correctly with this parameter, since the host or other clients may also perform the heal.\rHost - works only on host.\rHostAndClient - works on host and client.\r=配置工作模式：  \n**警告**：選擇`HostAndClient`需自行承擔風險，該模式可能在未來遊戲更新後失效。若其他大廳玩家不同意此參數，請勿使用。此外，`Percent`參數可能與此模式沖突，因主機或其他客戶端也可能執行治療。  \n\n**主機** - 僅主機生效  \n**主機與客戶端** - 主機和客戶端均生效\r
